###xml 349 373 349 373 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b35">Noben-Trauth <italic>et al.</italic> 1997</xref>
###xml 390 392 390 392 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">3J</sup>
###xml 394 418 394 418 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b30">McCullough &amp; Tempel 2004</xref>
###xml 421 426 421 426 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Spnb4</italic>
###xml 467 473 467 473 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">et al.</italic>
###xml 457 478 457 478 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b40">Parkinson <italic>et al.</italic> 2001</xref>
###xml 481 487 481 487 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Kcnj10</italic>
###xml 550 556 550 556 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">et al.</italic>
###xml 543 561 543 561 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b27">Marcus <italic>et al.</italic> 2002</xref>
###xml 570 576 570 576 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">et al.</italic>
###xml 563 581 563 581 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b34">Neusch <italic>et al.</italic> 2001</xref>
###xml 863 869 863 869 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">et al.</italic>
###xml 858 874 858 874 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b38">Ondo <italic>et al.</italic> 2003</xref>
###xml 967 972 967 972 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">SCN8A</italic>
###xml 982 988 982 988 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">et al.</italic>
###xml 974 993 974 993 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b46">Sharkey <italic>et al.</italic> 2008</xref>
###xml 1173 1179 1173 1179 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">et al.</italic>
###xml 1166 1184 1166 1184 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="b15">Gordon <italic>et al.</italic> 1995</xref>
###xml 1214 1219 1214 1219 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Scn8a</italic>
###xml 1219 1223 1219 1223 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Clth</italic>
###xml 1219 1223 1219 1223 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><italic>Clth</italic></sup>
###xml 1281 1284 1281 1284 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">SCN</italic>
###xml 1329 1334 1325 1330 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">SCN8A</italic>
###xml 1426 1431 1422 1427 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">SCN8A</italic>
###xml 14 19 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mouse</span>
###xml 141 146 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mouse</span>
###xml 226 230 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">OMIM</span>
###xml 604 608 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 679 684 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">human</span>
###xml 739 743 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">OMIM</span>
###xml 763 771 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">patients</span>
###xml 905 913 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">patients</span>
###xml 1121 1125 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">OMIM</span>
###xml 1224 1228 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 1236 1241 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">human</span>
###xml 1384 1390 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">humans</span>
###xml 1545 1551 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">humans</span>
The Scn8aClth mouse is a novel mutant that links peripheral neural hearing loss with tremor and paroxysmal motor symptoms. A small number of mouse mutants with continuous tremor and hearing impairment have been reported (MGI, OMIM), including several other ion channel mutants [Atp2b2 (plasma membrane calcium-transporting ATPase 2): deafwaddler2J (Noben-Trauth et al. 1997) and deafwaddler3J (McCullough & Tempel 2004); Spnb4 (spectrin beta 4): quivering (Parkinson et al. 2001); Kcnj10 (ATP-sensitive inward rectifier potassium channel 10) (Marcus et al. 2002; Neusch et al. 2001)]. However, no mutant mice with hearing loss and paroxysmal tremor have been reported. Around 12 human disorders feature both hearing impairment and tremor (OMIM). Essential tremor patients show significantly increased occurrence of high-frequency sensorineural hearing loss (Ondo et al. 2003); however, a recent screen of patients with essential tremor did not detect any variants of SCN8A (Sharkey et al. 2008). Sensorineural deafness and tremor are also seen in the autosomal dominant demyelinating Charcot-Marie-Tooth disease type 1E (OMIM) and in 18q deletion dystonia syndrome (Gordon et al. 1995). The paroxysmal symptoms in Scn8aClth mice and in human disorders caused by mutations in other SCNalpha-subunit genes suggest that mutation in SCN8A could also contribute to paroxysmal disorders in humans. It will be intriguing to consider SCN8A as a candidate gene for peripheral neural hearing loss and paroxysmal neurological or neuromuscular disorders in humans.
###end p 67
